<s> SABIN CHAPTER I A SUPPER PARTY AT THE "MILAN" </s>
<s> "To all such meetings as these" </s>
<s> cried Densham, lifting his champagne glass from under the soft halo of the rose-shaded electric lights </s>
<s> "Let us drink to them, Wolfenden--Mr Felix" </s>
<s> "To all such meetings" </s>
<s> echoed his _vis-� -vis_, also fingering the delicate stem of his glass </s>
<s> "An excellent toast" </s>
<s> "To all such meetings as these" </s>
<s> murmured the third man, who made up the little party </s>
<s> "A capital toast indeed" </s>
<s> They sat at a little round table in the brilliantly-lit supper-room of one of London's most fashionable restaurants </s>
<s> Around them were the usual throng of well dressed men, of women with bare shoulders and flashing diamonds, of dark-visaged waiters, deft, silent, swift-footed </s>
<s> The pleasant hum of conversation, louder and more unrestrained as the hour grew towards midnight, was varied by the popping of corks and many little trills of feminine laughter </s>
<s> Of discordant sounds there were none </s>
<s> The waiters' feet fell noiselessly upon the thick carpet, the clatter of plates was a thing unheard of </s>
<s> From the balcony outside came the low, sweet music of a German orchestra played by master hands </s>
<s> As usual the place was filled </s>
<s> Several late-comers, who had neglected to order their table beforehand, had already, after a disconsolate tour of the room, been led to one of the smaller apartments, or had driven off again to where the lights from the larger but less smart Altoné flashed out upon the smooth, dark waters of the Thames </s>
<s> Only one table was as yet unoccupied, and that was within a yard or two of the three young men who were celebrating a chance meeting in Pall Mall so pleasantly </s>
<s> It was laid for two only, and a magnificent bunch of white roses had, a few minutes before, been brought in and laid in front of one of the places by the director of the rooms himself </s>
<s> A man's small visiting-card was leaning against a wineglass </s>
<s> The table was evidently reserved by some one of importance, for several late-comers had pointed to it, only to be met by a decided shake of the head on the part of the waiter to whom they had appealed </s>
<s> As time went on, this empty table became the object of some speculation to the three young men </s>
<s> "Our neighbours," remarked Wolfenden, "are running it pretty fine </s>
<s> Can you see whose name is upon the card, Densham" </s>
<s> The man addressed raised an eyeglass to his left eye and leaned forward </s>
<s> Then he shook his head, he was a little too far away </s>
<s> "No </s>
<s> It is a short name </s>
<s> Seems to begin with S </s>
<s> Probably a son of Israel" </s>
<s> "His taste in flowers is at any rate irreproachable," Wolfenden remarked </s>
<s> "I wish they would come </s>
<s> I am in a genial mood, and I do not like to think of any one having to hurry over such an excellent supper" </s>
<s> "The lady," Densham suggested, "is probably theatrical, and has to dress after the show </s>
<s> Half-past twelve is a barbarous hour to turn us out </s>
<s> I wonder----" "Sh-sh" </s>
<s> The slight exclamation and a meaning frown from Wolfenden checked his speech </s>
<s> He broke off in the middle of his sentence, and looked round </s>
<s> There was the soft swish of silk passing his chair, and the faint suggestion of a delicate and perfectly strange perfume </s>
<s> At last the table was being taken possession of </s>
<s> A girl, in a wonderful white dress, was standing there, leaning over to admire the great bunch of creamy-white blossoms, whilst a waiter respectfully held a chair for her </s>
<s> A few steps behind came her companion, an elderly man who walked with a slight limp, leaning heavily upon a stick </s>
<s> She turned to him and made some remark in French, pointing to the flowers </s>
<s> He smiled, and passing her, stood for a moment leaning slightly upon the back of his chair, waiting, with a courtesy which was obviously instinctive, until she should have seated herself </s>
<s> During the few seconds which elapsed before they were settled in their places he glanced around the room with a smile, slightly cynical, but still good-natured, parting his thin, well-shaped lips </s>
<s> Wolfenden and Densham, who were looking at him with frank curiosity, he glanced at carelessly </s>
<s> The third young man of the party, Felix, was bending low over his plate, and his face was hidden </s>
<s> The buzz of conversation in their immediate vicinity had been temporarily suspended </s>
<s> Every one who had seen them enter had been interested in these late-comers, and many curious eyes had followed them to their seats </s>
<s> Briefly, the girl was beautiful and the man distinguished </s>
<s> When they had taken their places, however, the hum of conversation recommenced </s>
<s> Densham and Wolfenden leaned over to one another, and their questions were almost simultaneous </s>
<s> "Who are they" </s>
<s> "Who is she" </s>
<s> Alas </s>
<s> neither of them knew; neither of them had the least idea </s>
<s> Felix, Wolfenden's guest, it seemed useless to ask </s>
<s> He had only just arrived in England, and he was a complete stranger to London </s>
<s> Besides, he did not seem to be interested </s>
<s> He was proceeding calmly with his supper, with his back directly turned upon the new-comers </s>
<s> Beyond one rapid, upward glance at their entrance he seemed almost to have avoided looking at them </s>
<s> Wolfenden thought of this afterwards </s>
<s> "I see Harcutt in the corner," he said </s>
<s> "He will know who they are for certain </s>
<s> I shall go and ask him" </s>
<s> He crossed the room and chatted for a few minutes with a noisy little party in an adjacent recess </s>
<s> Presently he put his question </s>
<s> Alas </s>
<s> not one of them knew </s>
<s> Harcutt, a journalist of some note and a man who prided himself upon knowing absolutely everybody, was as helpless as the rest </s>
<s> To his humiliation he was obliged to confess it </s>
<s> "I never saw either of them before in my life," he said </s>
<s> "I cannot imagine who they can be </s>
<s> They are certainly foreigners" </s>
<s> "Very likely," Wolfenden agreed quietly </s>
<s> "In fact, I never doubted it </s>
<s> An English girl of that age--she is very young by the bye--would never be so perfectly turned out" </s>
<s> "What a very horrid thing to say, Lord Wolfenden," exclaimed the woman on whose chair his hand was resting </s>
<s> "Don't you know that dressing is altogether a matter of one's maid </s>
<s> You may rely upon it that that girl has found a treasure" </s>
<s> "Well, I don't know," Wolfenden said, smiling </s>
<s> "Young English girls always seem to me to look so dishevelled in evening dress </s>
<s> Now this girl is dressed with the art of a Frenchwoman of mature years, and yet with the simplicity of a child" </s>
<s> The woman laid down her lorgnettes and shrugged her shoulders </s>
<s> "I agree with you," she said, "that she is probably not English </s>
<s> If she were she would not wear such diamonds at her age" </s>
<s> "By the bye," Harcutt remarked with sudden cheerfulness, "we shall be able to find out who the man is when we leave </s>
<s> The table was reserved, so the name will be on the list at the door" </s>
<s> His friends rose to leave and Harcutt, making his adieux, crossed the room with Wolfenden </s>
<s> "We may as well have our coffee together," he said </s>
<s> "I ordered Turkish and I've been waiting for it ten minutes </s>
<s> We got here early </s>
<s> Hullo </s>
<s> where's your other guest" </s>
<s> Densham was sitting alone </s>
<s> Wolfenden looked at him inquiringly </s>
<s> "Your friend Felix has gone," he announced </s>
<s> "Suddenly remembered an engagement with his chief, and begged you to excuse him </s>
<s> Said he'd look you up to-morrow" </s>
<s> "Well, he's an odd fellow," Wolfenden remarked, motioning Harcutt to the vacant place </s>
<s> "His looks certainly belie his name" </s>
<s> "He's not exactly a cheerful companion for a supper party," Densham admitted, "but I like his face </s>
<s> How did you come across him, Wolfenden, and where does he hail from" </s>
<s> "He's a junior attaché at the Russian Embassy," Wolfenden said, stirring his coffee </s>
<s> "Only just been appointed </s>
<s> Charlie Meynell gave him a line of introduction to me; said he was a decent sort, but mopish </s>
<s> I looked him up last week, met him in Pall Mall just as you came along, and asked you both to supper </s>
<s> What liqueurs, Harcutt" </s>
<s> The conversation drifted into ordinary channels and flowed on steadily </s>
<s> At the same time it was maintained with a certain amount of difficulty </s>
<s> The advent of these two people at the next table had produced an extraordinary effect upon the three men </s>
<s> Harcutt was perhaps the least affected </s>
<s> He was a young man of fortune and natural gifts, who had embraced journalism as a career, and was really in love with his profession </s>
<s> Partly on account of his social position, which was unquestioned, and partly because his tastes tended in that direction, he had become the recognised scribe and chronicle of smart society </s>
<s> His pen was easy and fluent </s>
<s> He was an inimitable maker of short paragraphs </s>
<s> He prided himself upon knowing everybody and all about them </s>
<s> He could have told how much a year Densham, a rising young portrait painter, was making from his profession, and exactly what Wolfenden's allowance from his father was </s>
<s> A strange face was an annoyance to him; too, a humiliation </s>
<s> He had been piqued that he could not answer the eager questions of his own party as to these two people, and subsequently Wolfenden's inquiries </s>
<s> The thought that very soon at any rate their name would be known to him was, in a sense, a consolation </s>
<s> The rest would be easy </s>
<s> Until he knew all about them he meant to conceal so far as possible his own interest </s>
<s> CHAPTER II A DRAMA OF THE PAVEMENT The pitch of conversation had risen higher, still mingled with the intermittent popping of corks and the striking of matches </s>
<s> Blue wreaths of cigarette smoke were curling upwards--a delicate feeling of "abandon" was making itself felt amongst the roomful of people </s>
<s> The music grew softer as the babel of talk grew in volume </s>
<s> The whole environment became tinged with a faint but genial voluptuousness </s>
<s> Densham was laughing over the foibles of some mutual acquaintance; Wolfenden leaned back in his chair, smoking a cigarette and sipping his Turkish coffee </s>
<s> His eyes scarcely left for a moment the girl who sat only a few yards away from him, trifling with a certain dainty indifference with the little dishes, which one after the other had been placed before her and removed </s>
<s> He had taken pains to withdraw himself from the discussion in which his friends were interested </s>
<s> He wanted to be quite free to watch her </s>
<s> To him she was certainly the most wonderful creature he had ever seen </s>
<s> In every one of her most trifling actions she seemed possessed of an original and curious grace, even the way she held her silver fork, toyed with her serviette, raised her glass to her lips and set it down again--all these little things she seemed to him to accomplish with a peculiar and wonderful daintiness </s>
<s> Of conversation between her companion and herself there was evidently very little, nor did she appear to expect it </s>
<s> He was enjoying his supper with the moderation and minute care for trifles which denote the epicure, and he only spoke to her between the courses </s>
<s> She, on the other hand, appeared to be eating scarcely anything </s>
<s> At last, however, the waiter set before her a dish in which she was evidently interested </s>
<s> Wolfenden recognised the pink frilled paper and smiled </s>
<s> She was human enough then to care for ices </s>
<s> She bent over it and shrugged her shoulders--turning to the waiter who was hovering near, she asked a question </s>
<s> He bowed and removed the plate </s>
<s> In a moment or two he reappeared with another </s>
<s> This time the paper and its contents were brown </s>
<s> She smiled as she helped herself--such a smile that Wolfenden wondered that the waiter did not lose his head, and hand her pepper and salt instead of gravely filling her glass </s>
<s> She took up her spoon and deliberately tasted the contents of her plate </s>
<s> Then she looked across the table, and spoke the first words in English which he had heard from her lips-- "Coffee ice </s>
<s> So much nicer than strawberry" </s>
<s> The man nodded back </s>
<s> "Ices after supper are an abomination," he said </s>
<s> "They spoil the flavour of your wine, and many other things </s>
<s> But after all, I suppose it is waste of time to tell you so </s>
<s> A woman never understands how to eat until she is fifty" </s>
<s> She laughed, and deliberately finished the ice </s>
<s> Just as she laid down the spoon, she raised her eyes quietly and encountered Wolfenden's </s>
<s> He looked away at once with an indifference which he felt to be badly assumed </s>
<s> Did she know, he wondered, that he had been watching her like an owl all the time </s>
<s> He felt hot and uncomfortable--a veritable schoolboy at the thought </s>
<s> He plunged into the conversation between Harcutt and Densham--a conversation which they had been sustaining with an effort </s>
<s> They too were still as interested in their neighbours, although their positions at the table made it difficult for either to observe them closely </s>
<s> When three men are each thinking intently of something else, it is not easy to maintain an intelligent discussion </s>
<s> Wolfenden, to create a diversion, called for the bill </s>
<s> When he had paid it, and they were ready to depart, Densham looked up with a little burst of candour-- "She's wonderful" </s>
<s> he exclaimed softly </s>
<s> "Marvellous" </s>
<s> Wolfenden echoed </s>
<s> "I wonder who on earth they can possibly be," Harcutt said almost peevishly </s>
<s> Already he was being robbed of some part of his contemplated satisfaction </s>
<s> It was true that he would probably find the man's name on the table-list at the door, but he had a sort of presentiment that the girl's personality would elude him </s>
<s> The question of relationship between the man and the girl puzzled him </s>
<s> He propounded the problem and they discussed it with bated breath </s>
<s> There was no likeness at all </s>
<s> Was there any relationship </s>
<s> It was significant that although Harcutt was a scandalmonger and Wolfenden somewhat of a cynic, they discussed it with the most profound respect </s>
<s> Relationship after all of some sort there must be </s>
<s> What was it </s>
<s> It was Harcutt who alone suggested what to Wolfenden seemed an abominable possibility </s>
<s> "Scarcely husband and wife, I should think," he said thoughtfully, "yet one never can tell" </s>
<s> Involuntarily they all three glanced towards the man </s>
<s> He was well preserved and his little imperial and short grey moustache were trimmed with military precision, yet his hair was almost white, and his age could scarcely be less than sixty </s>
<s> In his way he was quite as interesting as the girl </s>
<s> His eyes, underneath his thick brows, were dark and clear, and his features were strong and delicately shaped </s>
<s> His hands were white and very shapely, the fingers were rather long, and he wore two singularly handsome rings, both set with strange stones </s>
<s> By the side of the table rested the stick upon which he had been leaning during his passage through the room </s>
<s> It was of smooth, dark wood polished like a malacca cane, and set at the top with a curious, green, opalescent stone, as large as a sparrow's egg </s>
<s> The eyes of the three men had each in turn been arrested by it </s>
<s> In the electric light which fell softly upon the upper part of it, the stone seemed to burn and glow with a peculiar, iridescent radiance </s>
<s> Evidently it was a precious possession, for once when a waiter had offered to remove it to a stand at the other end of the room, the man had stopped him sharply and drawn it a little closer towards him </s>
<s> Wolfenden lit a fresh cigarette, and gazed thoughtfully into the little cloud of blue smoke </s>
<s> "Husband and wife," he repeated slowly </s>
<s> "What an absurd idea </s>
<s> More likely father and daughter" </s>
<s> "How about the roses" </s>
<s> Harcutt remarked </s>
<s> "A father does not as a rule show such excellent taste in flowers" </s>
<s> They had finished supper </s>
<s> Suddenly the girl stretched out her left hand and took a glove from the table </s>
<s> Wolfenden smiled triumphantly </s>
<s> "She has no wedding-ring," he exclaimed softly </s>
<s> Then Harcutt, for the first time, made a remark for which he was never altogether forgiven--a remark which both the other men received in chilling silence </s>
<s> "That may or may not be a matter for congratulation," he said, twirling his moustache </s>
<s> "One never knows" </s>
<s> Wolfenden stood up, turning his back upon Harcutt and pointedly ignoring him </s>
<s> "Let us go, Densham," he said </s>
<s> "We are almost the last" </s>
<s> As a matter of fact his movement was made at exactly the right time </s>
<s> They could scarcely have left the room at the same moment as these two people, in whom manifestly they had been taking so great an interest </s>
<s> But by the time they had sent for their coats and hats from the cloak-room, and Harcutt had coolly scrutinised the table-list, they found themselves all together in a little group at the head of the stairs </s>
<s> Wolfenden, who was a few steps in front, drew back to allow them to pass </s>
<s> The man, leaning upon his stick, laid his hand upon the girl's sleeve </s>
<s> Then he looked up at the man, and addressed Wolfenden directly </s>
<s> "You had better precede us, sir," he said; "my progress is unfortunately somewhat slow" </s>
<s> Wolfenden drew back courteously </s>
<s> "We are in no hurry," he said </s>
<s> "Please go on" </s>
<s> The man thanked him, and with one hand upon the girl's shoulder and with the other on his stick commenced to descend </s>
<s> The girl had passed on without even glancing towards them </s>
<s> She had twisted a white lace mantilla around her head, and her features were scarcely visible--only as she passed, Wolfenden received a general impression of rustling white silk and lace and foaming tulle as she gathered her skirts together at the head of the stairs </s>
<s> It seemed to him, too, that the somewhat close atmosphere of the vestibule had become faintly sweet with the delicate fragrance of the white roses which hung by a loop of satin from her wrist </s>
<s> The three men waited until they had reached the bend of the stairs before they began to descend </s>
<s> Harcutt then leaned forward </s>
<s> "His name," he whispered, "is disenchanting </s>
<s> It is Mr Sabin </s>
<s> Whoever heard of a Mr Sabin </s>
<s> Yet he looks like a personage" </s>
<s> At the doors there was some delay </s>
<s> It was raining fast and the departures were a little congested </s>
<s> The three young men still kept in the background </s>
<s> Densham affected to be busy lighting a cigarette, Wolfenden was slowly drawing on his gloves </s>
<s> His place was almost in a line with the girl's </s>
<s> He could see the diamonds flashing in her fair hair through the dainty tracery of the drooping white lace, and in a moment, through some slight change in her position, he could get a better view of her face than he had been able to obtain even in the supper-room </s>
<s> She was beautiful </s>
<s> There was no doubt about that </s>
<s> But there were many beautiful women in London, whom Wolfenden scarcely pretended to admire </s>
<s> This girl had something better even than supreme beauty </s>
<s> She was anything but a reproduction </s>
<s> She was a new type </s>
<s> She had originality </s>
<s> Her hair was dazzlingly fair; her eyebrows, delicately arched, were high and distinctly dark in colour </s>
<s> Her head was perfectly shaped--the features seemed to combine a delightful piquancy with a somewhat statuesque regularity </s>
<s> Wolfenden, wondering of what she in some manner reminded him, suddenly thought of some old French miniatures, which he had stopped to admire only a day or two before, in a little curio shop near Bond Street </s>
<s> There was a distinct dash of something foreign in her features and carriage </s>
<s> It might have been French, or Austrian--it was most certainly not Anglo-Saxon </s>
<s> The crush became a little less, they all moved a step or two forward--and Wolfenden, glancing carelessly outside, found his attention immediately arrested </s>
<s> Just as he had been watching the girl, so was a man, who stood on the pavement side by side with the commissionaire, watching her companion </s>
<s> He was tall and thin; apparently dressed in evening clothes, for though his coat was buttoned up to his chin, he wore an opera hat </s>
<s> His hands were thrust into the loose pockets of his overcoat, and his face was mostly in the shadows </s>
<s> Once, however, he followed some motion of Mr Sabin's and moved his head a little forward </s>
<s> Wolfenden started and looked at him fixedly </s>
<s> Was it fancy, or was there indeed something clenched in his right hand there, which gleamed like silver--or was it steel--in the momentary flash of a passing carriage-light </s>
<s> Wolfenden was puzzled </s>
<s> There was something, too, which seemed to him vaguely familiar in the man's figure and person </s>
<s> He was certainly waiting for somebody, and to judge from his expression his mission was no pleasant one </s>
<s> Wolfenden who, through the latter part of the evening, had felt a curious and unwonted sense of excitement stirring his blood, now felt it go tingling through all his veins </s>
<s> He had some subtle prescience that he was on the brink of an adventure </s>
<s> He glanced hurriedly at his two companions; neither of them had noticed this fresh development </s>
<s> Just then the commissionaire, who knew Wolfenden by sight, turned round and saw him standing there </s>
<s> Stepping back on to the pavement, he called up the brougham, which was waiting a little way down the street </s>
<s> "Your carriage, my lord," he said to Wolfenden, touching his cap </s>
<s> Wolfenden, with ready presence of mind, shook his head </s>
<s> "I am waiting for a friend," he said </s>
<s> "Tell my man to pass on a yard or two" </s>
<s> The man bowed, and the danger of leaving before these two people, in whom his interest now was becoming positively feverish, was averted </s>
<s> As if to enhance it, a singular thing now happened </s>
<s> The interest suddenly became reciprocal </s>
<s> At the sound of Wolfenden's voice the man with the club foot had distinctly started </s>
<s> He changed his position and, leaning forward, looked eagerly at him </s>
<s> His eyes remained for a moment or two fixed steadily upon him </s>
<s> There was no doubt about the fact, singular in itself though it was </s>
<s> Wolfenden noticed it himself, so did both Densham and Harcutt </s>
<s> But before any remark could pass between them a little _coupé_ brougham had drawn up, and the man and the girl started forward </s>
<s> Wolfenden followed close behind </s>
<s> The feeling which prompted him to do so was a curious one, but it seemed to him afterwards that he had even at that time a conviction that something unusual was about to happen </s>
<s> The girl stepped lightly across the carpeted way and entered the carriage </s>

<s> CHAPTER XII WOLFENDEN'S LUCK To leave London at all, under ordinary circumstances, was usually a hardship for Wolfenden, but to leave London at this particular moment of his life was little less than a calamity, yet a letter which he received a few mornings after the supper at the "Milan" left him scarcely any alternative </s>
<s> He read it over for the third time whilst his breakfast grew cold, and each time his duty seemed to become plainer </s>
<s> "DERINGHAM HALL, NORFOLK </s>
<s> "MY DEAR WOLFENDEN,--We have been rather looking for you to come down for a day or two, and I do hope that you will be able to manage it directly you receive this </s>
<s> I am sorry to say that your father is very far from well, and we have all been much upset lately </s>
<s> He still works for eight or nine hours a day, and his hallucinations as to the value of his papers increases with every page he writes </s>
<s> His latest peculiarity is a rooted conviction that there is some plot on hand to rob him of his manuscripts </s>
<s> You remember, perhaps, Miss Merton, the young person whom we engaged as typewriter </s>
<s> He sent her away the other day, without a moment's notice, simply because he saw her with a sheet of copying paper in her hand </s>
<s> I did not like the girl, but it is perfectly ridiculous to suspect her of anything of the sort </s>
<s> He insisted, however, that she should leave the house within an hour, and we were obliged to give in to him </s>
<s> Since then he has seemed to become even more fidgety </s>
<s> He has had cast-iron shutters fitted to the study windows, and two of the keepers are supposed to be on duty outside night and day, with loaded revolvers </s>
<s> People around here are all beginning to talk, and I am afraid that it is only natural that they should </s>
<s> He will see no one, and the library door is shut and bolted immediately he has entered it </s>
<s> Altogether it is a deplorable state of things, and what will be the end of it I cannot imagine </s>
<s> Sometimes it occurs to me that you might have more influence over him than I have </s>
<s> I hope that you will be able to come down, if only for a day or two, and see what effect your presence has </s>
<s> The shooting is not good this year, but Captain Willis was telling me yesterday that the golf links were in excellent condition, and there is the yacht, of course, if you care to use it </s>
<s> Your father seems to have quite forgotten that she is still in the neighbourhood, I am glad to say </s>
<s> Those inspection cruises were very bad things for him </s>
<s> He used to get so excited, and he was dreadfully angry if the photographs which I took were at all imperfectly developed </s>
<s> How is everybody </s>
<s> Have you seen Lady Susan lately </s>
<s> and is it true that Eleanor is engaged </s>

<s> London, for him at present, would be madness </s>
<s> I shall hope to get a wire from you to-morrow, and will send to Cromer to meet any train.--From your affectionate mother, "CONSTANCE MANVER DERINGHAM" </s>
<s> There was not a word of reproach in the letter, but nevertheless Wolfenden felt a little conscience-stricken </s>

<s> It was true that he could not call upon them, and he had no idea where else to look for these people, who, for some mysterious reason, seemed to be doing all that they could to avoid his acquaintance </s>

<s> He had become a saunterer, and the shop windows had obtained from him an attention which he had never previously bestowed upon them </s>

<s> CHAPTER XIII A GREAT WORK The Countess of Deringham might be excused for considering herself the most unfortunate woman in England </s>
<s> In a single week she had passed from the position of one of the most brilliant leaders of English society to be the keeper of a recluse, whose sanity was at least doubtful </s>
<s> Her husband, Admiral the Earl of Deringham, had been a man of iron nerve and constitution, with a splendid reputation, and undoubtedly a fine seaman </s>
<s> The horror of a single day had broken up his life </s>
<s> He had been the awe-stricken witness of a great naval catastrophe, in which many of his oldest friends and companions had gone to the bottom of the sea before his eyes, together with nearly a thousand British seamen </s>
<s> The responsibility for the disaster lay chiefly from those who had perished in it, yet some small share of the blame was fastened upon the onlookers, and he himself, as admiral in command, had not altogether escaped </s>
<s> From the moment when they had led him down from the bridge of his flagship, grey and fainting, he had been a changed man </s>
<s> He had never recovered from the shock </s>
<s> He retired from active service at once, under a singular and marvellously persistent delusion </s>
<s> Briefly he believed, or professed to believe, that half the British fleet had perished, and that the country was at the mercy of the first great Power who cared to send her warships up the Thames </s>
<s> It was a question whether he was really insane; on any ordinary topic his views were the views of a rational man, but the task which he proceeded to set himself was so absorbing that any other subject seemed scarcely to come within the horizon of his comprehension </s>
<s> He imagined himself selected by no less a person than the Secretary for War, to devote the rest of his life to the accomplishment of a certain undertaking </s>
<s> Practically his mission was to prove by figures, plans, and naval details (unknown to the general public), the complete helplessness of the empire </s>
<s> He bought a yacht and commenced a series of short cruises, lasting over two years, during the whole of which time his wife was his faithful and constant companion </s>
<s> They visited in turn each one of the fortified ports of the country, winding up with a general inspection of every battleship and cruiser within British waters </s>
<s> Then, with huge piles of amassed information before him, he settled down in Norfolk to the framing of his report, still under the impression that the whole country was anxiously awaiting it </s>
<s> His wife remained with him then, listening daily to the news of his progress, and careful never to utter a single word of discouragement or disbelief in the startling facts which he sometimes put before her </s>
<s> The best room in the house, the great library, was stripped perfectly bare and fitted up for his study, and a typist was engaged to copy out the result of his labours in fair form </s>
<s> Lately, the fatal results to England which would follow the public disclosure of her awful helplessness had weighed heavily upon him, and he was beginning to live in the fear of betrayal </s>
<s> The room in which he worked was fitted with iron shutters, and was guarded night and day </s>
<s> He saw no visitors, and was annoyed if any were permitted to enter the house </s>
<s> He met his wife only at dinner time, for which meal he dressed in great state, and at which no one else was ever allowed to be present </s>
<s> He suffered, when they were alone, no word to pass his lips, save with reference to the subject of his labours; it is certain he looked upon himself as the discoverer of terrible secrets </s>

<s> If he heard it he did not reply </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXI HARCUTT'S INSPIRATION Wolfenden lost his match upon the last hole; nevertheless it was a finely contested game, and when Mr Sabin proposed a round on the following day, he accepted without hesitation </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXII FROM THE BEGINNING A woman stood, in the midst of a salt wilderness, gazing seaward </s>
<s> Around her was a long stretch of wet sand and of seaweed-stained rocks, rising from little pools of water left by the tide; and beyond, the flat, marshy country was broken only by that line of low cliffs, from which the little tufts of grass sprouted feebly </s>
<s> The waves which rolled almost to her feet were barely ripples, breaking with scarcely a visible effort upon the moist sand </s>
<s> Above, the sky was grey and threatening; only a few minutes before a cloud of white mist had drifted in from the sea and settled softly upon the land in the form of rain </s>
<s> The whole outlook was typical of intense desolation </s>
<s> The only sound breaking the silence, almost curiously devoid of all physical and animal noises, was the soft washing of the sand at her feet, and every now and then the jingling of silver harness, as the horses of her carriage, drawn up on the road above, tossed their heads and fidgeted </s>
<s> The carriage itself seemed grotesquely out of place </s>
<s> The coachman, with powdered hair and the dark blue Deringham livery, sat perfectly motionless, his head bent a little forward, and his eyes fixed upon his horses' ears </s>
<s> The footman, by their side, stood with folded arms, and expression as wooden as though he were waiting upon a Bond Street pavement </s>
<s> Both were weary, and both would have liked to vary the monotony by a little conversation; but only a few yards away the woman was standing whose curious taste had led her to visit such a spot </s>

<s> Something about her attitude bespoke a keen and intimate sympathy with the desolation of her surroundings </s>
<s> The woman was unhappy; the light in her dark eyes was inimitably sad </s>
<s> Her cheeks were pale and a little wan </s>

<s> Her figure was still slim and elegant, the streaks of grey in her raven black hair were few and far between </s>
<s> She might have lived hand in hand with sorrow, but it had done very little to age her </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXV A HANDFUL OF ASHES The Countess of Deringham was sitting alone in her smaller drawing-room, gazing steadfastly at a certain spot in the blazing fire before her </s>
<s> A little pile of grey ashes was all that remained of the sealed packet which she had placed within the bars only a few seconds ago </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXXV A LITTLE GAME OF CARDS Mr Sabin, whose carriage had set him down at the Cromer railway station with barely two minutes to spare, took his seat in an empty first-class smoking carriage of the London train and deliberately lit a fine cigar </s>
<s> He was filled with that sense of triumphant self-satisfaction which falls to the lot of a man who, after much arduous labour successfully accomplished, sees very near at hand the great desire of his life </s>
<s> Two days' more quiet work, and his task was done </s>
<s> All that he had pledged himself to give, he would have ready for the offering </s>
<s> The finishing touches were but a matter of detail </s>
<s> It had been a great undertaking--more difficult at times than he had ever reckoned for </s>
<s> He told himself with some complacency that no other man breathing could have brought it to so satisfactory a conclusion </s>
<s> His had been a life of great endeavours; this one, however, was the crowning triumph of his career </s>
<s> He watched the people take their seats in the train with idle eyes; he was not interested in any of them </s>
<s> He scarcely saw their faces; they were not of his world nor he of theirs </s>
<s> But suddenly he received a rude shock </s>
<s> He sat upright and wiped away the moisture from the window in order that he might see more clearly </s>
<s> A young man in a long ulster was buying newspapers from a boy only a yard or two away </s>
<s> Something about the figure and manner of standing seemed to Mr Sabin vaguely familiar </s>
<s> He waited until his head was turned, and the eyes of the two men met--then the last vestige of doubt disappeared </s>
<s> It was Felix </s>
<s> Mr Sabin leaned back in his corner with darkening face </s>
<s> He had noticed to his dismay that the encounter, surprising though it had been to him, had been accepted by Felix as a matter of course--he was obviously prepared for it </s>
<s> He had met Mr Sabin's anxious and incredulous gaze with a faint, peculiar smile </s>
<s> His probable presence in the train had evidently been confidently reckoned upon </s>
<s> Felix had been watching him secretly, and knowing what he did know of that young man, Mr Sabin was seriously disturbed </s>
<s> He did not hesitate for a moment, however, to face the position </s>
<s> He determined at once upon a bold course of action </s>
<s> Letting down the window he put out his head </s>
<s> "Are you going to town" </s>
<s> he asked Felix, as though seeing him then was the most natural thing in the world </s>
<s> The young man nodded </s>
<s> "Yes, it's getting pretty dreary down here, isn't it </s>
<s> You're off back, I see" </s>
<s> Mr Sabin assented </s>
<s> "Yes," he said, "I've had about enough of it </s>
<s> Besides, I'm overdue at Pau, and I'm anxious to get there </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXXIX THE HEART OF THE PRINCESS When Wolfenden opened his paper on Saturday morning, London had already drawn a great breath, partly of relief partly of surprise, for the black head-lines which topped the columns of the papers, the placards in the streets, and the cry of the newsboys, all declared a most remarkable change in the political situation </s>

<s> CHAPTER XL THE WAY TO PAU The way to Pau which Mr Sabin chose may possibly have been the most circuitous, but it was certainly the safest </s>
<s> Although not a muscle of his face had moved, although he had not by any physical movement or speech betrayed his knowledge of the fact, he was perfectly well aware that his little statement as to his future movements was overheard and carefully noted by the tall, immaculately dressed young man who by some strange chance seemed to have been at his elbow since he had left his rooms an hour ago </s>

<s> WATSON OF NEW YORK It was their third day out, and Mr Sabin was enjoying the voyage very much indeed </s>
<s> The _Calipha_ was a small boat sailing to Boston instead of New York, and contemptuously termed by the ocean-going public an old tub </s>

<s> CHAPTER XLVII A CHARMED LIFE The night was still enough, but piled-up masses of black clouds obscured a weakly moon, and there were only now and then uncertain gleams of glimmering light </s>
<s> There was no fog, nor any sign of any </s>

<s> CHAPTER L A HARBOUR TRAGEDY The voyage of the _Calipha_ came to its usual termination about ten o'clock on the following morning, when she passed Boston lights and steamed slowly down the smooth waters of the harbour </s>

<s> CHAPTER LI THE PERSISTENCE OF FELIX Of all unhappy men he is assuredly the most unhappy who, ambitious, patient, and doggedly persevering, has chosen the moment to make his supreme venture and having made it has reaped failure instead of success </s>
<s> The gambler while he lives may play again; the miser, robbed, embark once more upon his furtive task of hoarding money; even the rejected lover need not despair of some day, somewhere finding happiness, since no one heart has a monopoly of love </s>
<s> But to him who aspires to shape the destiny of nations, to control the varying interests of great powers and play upon the emotions of whole peoples, there is never vouchsafed more than one opportunity </s>
<s> And failure then does more than bring upon the schemer the execration of the world he would have controlled: it clears eyes into which he had thrown dust, awakens passions he had lulled to sleep, provokes hostility where he had made false peace, and renders for ever impossible the recombination of conditions under which alone he could, if at all, succeed </s>
<s> For such an one life has lost all its savour </s>
<s> Existence may perhaps be permitted to him, but no more </s>
<s> He stakes his all upon one single venture, and, win or lose, he has no second throw </s>
<s> Failure is absolute, and spells despair </s>
<s> In such unhappy state was Mr Sabin </s>
<s> More than ten days had passed since the tragedy in Boston Harbour, and now he sat alone in a private room in a small but exclusive hotel in New York </s>

<s> JAMES B </s>

<s> Mr Sabin found himself late on the afternoon of the following day alone on the platform of a little wooden station, watching the train which had dropped him there a few minutes ago snorting away round a distant curve </s>
<s> Outside, the servant whom he had hired that morning in New York was busy endeavouring to arrange for a conveyance of some sort in which they might complete their journey </s>
<s> Mr Sabin himself was well content to remain where he was </s>
<s> The primitiveness of the place itself and the magnificence of his surroundings had made a distinct and favourable impression upon him </s>
<s> Facing him was a chain of lofty hills whose foliage, luxuriant and brilliantly tinted, seemed almost like a long wave of rich deep colour, the country close at hand was black with pine trees, through which indeed a winding way for the railroad seemed to have been hewn </s>
<s> It was only a little clearing which had been made for the depôt; a few yards down, the line seemed to vanish into a tunnel of black foliage, from amongst which the red barked tree trunks stood out with the regularity of a regiment of soldiers </s>
<s> The clear air was fragrant with a peculiar and aromatic perfume, so sweet and wholesome that Mr Sabin held the cigarette which he had lighted at arm's length, that he might inhale this, the most fascinating odour in the world </s>
<s> He was at all times sensitive to the influence of scenery and natural perfumes, and the possibility of spending the rest of his days in this country had never seemed so little obnoxious as during those few moments </s>
<s> Then his eyes suddenly fell upon a large white house, magnificent, but evidently newly finished, gleaming forth from an opening in the woods, and his brows contracted </s>
<s> His former moodiness returned </s>
<s> "It is not the country," he muttered to himself, "it is the people" </s>
<s> His servant came back presently, with explanations for his prolonged absence </s>
<s> "I am sorry, sir," he said, "but I made a mistake in taking the tickets" </s>
<s> Mr Sabin merely nodded </s>
<s> A little time ago a mistake on the part of a servant was a thing which he would not have tolerated </s>
<s> But those were days which seemed to him to lie very far back in the past </s>
<s> "You ought to have alighted at the last station, sir," the man continued </s>
<s> "Stockbridge is eleven miles from here" </s>
<s> "What are we going to do" </s>
<s> Mr Sabin asked </s>
<s> "We must drive, sir </s>
<s> I have hired a conveyance, but the luggage will have to come later in the day by the cars </s>
<s> There will only be room for your dressing-bag in the buggy" </s>
<s> Mr Sabin rose to his feet </s>
<s> "The drive will be pleasant," he said, "especially if it is through such country as this </s>
<s> I am not sure that I regret your mistake, Harrison </s>
<s> You will remain and bring the baggage on, I suppose" </s>
<s> "It will be best, sir," the man agreed </s>
<s> "There is a train in about an hour" </s>
<s> They walked out on to the road where a one-horse buggy was waiting </s>
<s> The driver took no more notice of them than to terminate, in a leisurely way, his conversation with a railway porter, and unhitch the horse </s>
<s> Mr Sabin took the seat by his side, and they drove off </s>
<s> It was a very beautiful road, and Mr Sabin was quite content to lean back in his not uncomfortable seat and admire the scenery </s>
<s> For the most part it was of a luxuriant and broken character </s>
<s> There were very few signs of agriculture, save in the immediate vicinity of the large newly-built houses which they passed every now and then </s>
<s> At times they skirted the side of a mountain, and far below them in the valley the river Leine wound its way along like a broad silver band </s>
<s> Here and there the road passed through a thick forest of closely-growing pines, and Mr Sabin, holding his cigarette away from him, leaned back and took long draughts of the rosinous, piney odour </s>
<s> It was soon after emerging from the last of these that they suddenly came upon a house which moved Mr Sabin almost to enthusiasm </s>
<s> It lay not far back from the road, a very long two-storied white building, free from the over-ornamentation which disfigured most of the surrounding mansions </s>
<s> White pillars in front, after the colonial fashion, supported a long sloping veranda roof, and the smooth trimly-kept lawns stretched almost to the terrace which bordered the piazza </s>
<s> There were sun blinds of striped holland to the southern windows, and about the whole place there was an air of simple and elegant refinement, which Mr Sabin found curiously attractive </s>
<s> He broke for the first time the silence which had reigned between him and the driver </s>
<s> "Do you know," he inquired, "whose house that is" </s>
<s> The man flipped his horse's ears with the whip </s>
<s> "I guess so," he answered </s>
<s> "That is the old Peterson House </s>
<s> Mrs James B </s>
<s> Peterson lives there now" </s>
<s> Mr Sabin felt in his breast pocket, and extracted therefrom a letter </s>
<s> It was a coincidence undoubtedly, but the fact was indisputable </s>
<s> The address scrawled thereon in Felix's sprawling hand was:-- "MRS </s>
<s> JAMES B </s>
<s> PETERSON, "Lenox </s>
<s> "By favour of Mr Sabin" </s>
<s> "I will make a call there," Mr Sabin said to the man </s>
<s> "Drive me up to the house" </s>
<s> The man pulled up his horse </s>
<s> "What, do you know her" </s>
<s> he asked </s>
<s> Mr Sabin affected to be deeply interested in a distant point of the landscape </s>
<s> The man muttered something to himself and turned up the drive </s>
<s> "You have met her abroad, maybe" </s>
<s> he suggested </s>
<s> Mr Sabin took absolutely no notice of the question </s>
<s> The man's impertinence was too small a thing to annoy him, but it prevented his asking several questions which he would like to have had answered </s>
<s> The man muttered something about a civil answer to a civil question not being much to expect, and pulled up his horse in front of the great entrance porch </s>
<s> Mr Sabin, calmly ignoring him, descended and stepped through the wide open door into a beautiful square hall in the centre of which was a billiard table </s>
<s> A servant attired in unmistakably English livery, stepped forward to meet him </s>
<s> "Is Mrs Peterson at home" </s>
<s> Mr Sabin inquired </s>
<s> "We expect her in a very few minutes," the man answered </s>
<s> "She is out riding at present </s>
<s> May I inquire if you are Mr Sabin, sir" </s>
<s> Mr Sabin admitted the fact with some surprise </s>
<s> The man received the intimation with respect </s>
<s> "Will you kindly walk this way, your Grace," he said </s>
<s> Mr Sabin followed him into a large and delightfully furnished library </s>
<s> Then he looked keenly at the servant </s>
<s> "You know me," he remarked </s>
<s> "Monsieur Le Duc Souspennier," the man answered with a bow </s>
<s> "I am an Englishman, but I was in the service of the Marquis de la Merle in Paris for ten years" </s>
<s> "Your face," Mr Sabin said, "was familiar to me </s>
<s> You look like a man to be trusted </s>
<s> Will you be so good as to remember that the Duc is unfortunately dead, and I am Mr Sabin" </s>
<s> "Most certainly, sir," the man answered </s>
<s> "Is there anything which I can bring you" </s>
<s> "Nothing, thank you," Mr Sabin answered </s>
<s> The man withdrew with a low bow, and Mr Sabin stood for a few minutes turning over magazines and journals which covered a large round table, and represented the ephemeral literature of nearly every country in Europe </s>
<s> "Mrs Peterson," he remarked to himself, "must be a woman of Catholic tastes </s>
<s> Here is the _Le Petit Journal_ inside the pages of the English _Contemporary Review_" </s>
<s> He was turning the magazines over with interest, when he chanced to glance through the great south window a few feet away from him </s>
<s> Something he saw barely a hundred yards from the little iron fence which bordered the lawns, attracted his attention </s>
<s> He rubbed his eyes and looked at it again </s>
<s> He was puzzled, and was on the point of ringing the bell when the man who had admitted him entered, bearing a tray with liqueurs and cigarettes </s>
<s> Mr Sabin beckoned him over to the window </s>
<s> "What is that little flag" </s>
<s> he asked </s>
<s> "It is connected, I believe, in some way," the man answered, "with a game of which Mrs Peterson is very fond </s>
<s> I believe that it indicates the locality of a small hole" </s>
<s> "Golf" </s>
<s> Mr Sabin exclaimed </s>
<s> "That is the name of the game, sir," the man answered </s>
<s> "I had forgotten it for the moment" </s>
<s> Mr Sabin tried the window </s>
<s> "I want to get out," he said </s>
<s> The man opened it </s>
<s> "If you are going down there, sir," he said, "I will send James Green to meet you </s>
<s> Mrs Peterson is so fond of the game that she keeps a Scotchman here to look after the links and instruct her" </s>
<s> "This," Mr Sabin murmured, "is the most extraordinary thing in the world" </s>
<s> "If you would like to see your room, sir, before you go out," the man suggested, "it is quite ready </s>
<s> If you will give me your keys I will have your clothes laid out" </s>
<s> Mr Sabin turned about in amazement </s>
<s> "What do you mean" </s>
<s> he exclaimed </s>
<s> "I have not come here to stay" </s>
<s> "I understood so, sir," the man answered </s>
<s> "Your room has been ready for three weeks" </s>
<s> Mr Sabin was bewildered </s>
<s> Then he remembered the stories which he had heard of American hospitality, and concluded that this must be an instance of it </s>
<s> "I had not the slightest intention of stopping here," he said to the man </s>
<s> "Mrs Peterson expected you to do so, sir, and we have sent your conveyance away </s>
<s> If it is inconvenient for you to remain now, it will be easy to send you anywhere you desire later" </s>
<s> "For the immediate present," Mr Sabin said, "Mrs Peterson not having arrived, I want to see that golf course" </s>
<s> "If you will permit me, sir," the man said, "I will show you the way" </s>
<s> They followed a winding footpath which brought them suddenly out on the border of a magnificent stretch of park-like country </s>
<s> Mr Sabin, whose enthusiasms were rare, failed wholly to restrain a little exclamation of admiration </s>
<s> A few yards away was one of the largest and most magnificently kept putting-greens that he had ever seen in his life </s>
<s> By his side was a raised teeing-ground, well and solidly built </s>
<s> Far away down in the valley he could see the flag of the first hole just on the other side of a broad stream </s>
<s> "The gentleman's a golf-player, maybe" </s>
<s> remarked a voice by his side, in familiar dialect </s>
<s> Mr Sabin turned around to find himself confronted by a long, thin Scotchman, who had strolled out of a little shed close at hand </s>
<s> "I am very fond of the game," Mr Sabin admitted </s>
<s> "You appear to me to have a magnificent course here" </s>
<s> "It's none so bad," Mr James Green admitted </s>
<s> "Maybe the gentleman would like a round" </s>
<s> "There is nothing in this wide world," Mr Sabin answered truthfully, "that I should like so well </s>
<s> But I have no clubs or any shoes" </s>
<s> "Come this way, sir, come this way," was the prompt reply </s>
<s> "There's clubs here of all sorts such as none but Jimmy Green can make, ay, and shoes too </s>
<s> Mr Wilson, will you be sending me two boys down from the house" </s>
<s> In less than ten minutes Mr Sabin was standing upon the first tee, a freshly lit cigarette in his mouth, and a new gleam of enthusiasm in his eyes </s>
<s> He modestly declined the honour, and Mr Green forthwith drove a ball which he watched approvingly </s>
<s> "That's no such a bad ball," he remarked </s>
<s> Mr Sabin watched the construction of his tee, and swung his club lightly </s>
<s> "Just a little sliced, wasn't it" </s>
<s> he said </s>
<s> "That will do, thanks" </s>
<s> He addressed his ball with a confidence which savoured almost of carelessness, swung easily back and drove a clean, hard hit ball full seventy yards further than the professional </s>
<s> The man for a moment was speechless with surprise, and he gave a little gasp </s>
<s> "Aye, mon," he exclaimed </s>
<s> "That was a fine drive </s>
<s> Might you be having a handicap, sir" </s>
<s> "I am scratch at three clubs," Mr Sabin answered quietly, "and plus four at one" </s>
<s> A gleam of delight mingled with respect at his opponent, shone in the Scotchman's face </s>
<s> "Aye, but we will be having a fine game," he exclaimed </s>
<s> "Though I'm thinking you will down me </s>
<s> But it is grand good playing with a mon again" </s>
<s> * * * * * The match was now at the fifteenth hole </s>
<s> Mr Sabin, with a long and deadly putt--became four up and three to play </s>
<s> As the ball trickled into the hole the Scotchman drew a long breath </s>
<s> "It's a fine match," he said, "and I'm properly downed </s>
<s> What's more, you're holding the record of the links up to this present </s>
<s> Fifteen holes for sixty-four is verra good--verra good indeed </s>
<s> There's no man in America to-day to beat it" </s>
<s> And then Mr Sabin, who was on the point of making a genial reply, felt a sudden and very rare emotion stir his heart and blood, for almost in his ears there had sounded a very sweet and familiar voice, perhaps the voice above all others which he had least expected to hear again in this world </s>
<s> "You have not then forgotten your golf, Mr Sabin </s>
<s> What do you think of my little course" </s>
<s> He turned slowly round and faced her </s>
<s> She was standing on the rising ground just above the putting-green, the skirt of her riding habit gathered up in her hand, her lithe, supple figure unchanged by time, the old bewitching smile still playing about her lips </s>
<s> She was still the most beautiful woman he had ever seen </s>

<s> "I did not know it," he answered, gravely, "for I never heard of your marriage" </s>

<s> "It is very beautiful indeed," she said, "but it is very lonely" </s>

<s> he inquired </s>
